Crowd sourcing arrangements in which people are asked to contribute money in exchange for potential profits based on the work of others are considered to be securities.\r\n\r\n\r\nP2P Interest rates - One of the main advantages of person-to-person lending for borrowers can sometimes be better rates than traditional bank rates can offer. Because past behavior is frequently indicative of future performance and low credit scores correlate with high likelihood of default, peer-to-peer intermediaries have started to decline a large number of applicants and charge higher interest rates to riskier borrowers that are approved.
